class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">Notion maintains a comprehensive privacy compliance program and is This page highlights some of the key aspects of our program.</p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><div class="contentfulRichText_titleSpacingH2__yu1dl" id="how-we-handle-your-data"><h2 class="title_title__DWL5N title_titleSizeM__e46NM title_titleWeightBold__838EK title_titleFamilyInter__Ra6_Q"><a class="contentfulRichText_titleCursor__edkrn" href="/help/privacy#how-we-handle-your-data">How we handle your data</a><span class="contentfulRichText_permalink__tawv_"><svg class="link" viewBox="0 0 14 14" style="width:18px;height:18px;display:block;fill:inherit;flex-shrink:0"><path d="M7.03955 9.77881L7.93018 8.88232C7.22705 8.81787 6.73486 8.59521 6.37158 8.23193C5.38135 7.2417 5.38135 5.83545 fill="currentColor"></path></svg></span></h2></div></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">At Notion<strong class="contentfulRichText_strong__MaH0M">,</strong> our team is dedicated to developing and implementing data privacy processes and safeguards that meet industry standards and best practices. We conduct ongoing training for our teams to ensure that they are up to speed with developments in legislation and essential privacy and security practices. </p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">Every Notion employee and contractor signs up to non-disclosure terms to maintain the confidentiality and security of your data. Notion also holds any vendors that handle personal data to the same data management, security, and privacy practices and standards to which we hold ourselves.</p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><div class="contentfulRichText_titleSpacingH3__wUQTI"><h3 id="what-is-customer-data" class="title_title__DWL5N title_titleSizeS__om4Io title_titleWeightSemibold__RAo21 title_titleFamilyInter__Ra6_Q"><strong class="contentfulRichText_strong__MaH0M">What is Customer Data?</strong></h3></div></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">Notion defines Customer Data as any data that a customer stores in the Notion services. This can include personal information. </p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">Customer data does not include analytics data or Account Information, which we describe below. The terms of the Notion <a href="https://www.notion.so/notion/Master-Subscription-Agreement-4e1c5dd3e3de45dfa4a8ed60f1a43da0" class="InlineTextLink_inlineLink__oN8YM InlineTextLink_colorInherit__oGlTG">MSA</a> and Notion <a href="https://www.notion.so/notion/Data-Processing-Addendum-361b540101274b1fa7e16b90402b0d99" class="InlineTextLink_inlineLink__oN8YM InlineTextLink_colorInherit__oGlTG">DPA</a> apply to your Customer Data.</p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><div class="contentfulRichText_titleSpacingH3__wUQTI"><h3 id="what-is-account-information" class="title_title__DWL5N title_titleSizeS__om4Io title_titleWeightSemibold__RAo21 title_titleFamilyInter__Ra6_Q"><strong class="contentfulRichText_strong__MaH0M">What is Account Information?</strong></h3></div></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">Account information is the information that our customers provide to us so that we can create and administer their customer accounts. </p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">For example, account information includes names, usernames, passwords, phone numbers, email addresses, Workspace metadata, support communications, billing information, and usage information associated with your Notion account. </p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">The terms of the Notion <a href="https://www.notion.so/notion/Privacy-Policy-3468d120cf614d4c9014c09f6adc9091" class="InlineTextLink_inlineLink__oN8YM InlineTextLink_colorInherit__oGlTG">Privacy Policy</a> apply to any personal information included in Account Information.</p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><div class="contentfulRichText_titleSpacingH3__wUQTI"><h3 id="who-owns-and-controls-customer-data" class="title_title__DWL5N title_titleSizeS__om4Io title_titleWeightSemibold__RAo21 title_titleFamilyInter__Ra6_Q"><strong class="contentfulRichText_strong__MaH0M">Who owns and controls Customer Data?</strong></h3></div></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">You own your Customer Data, including any content you submit or upload to the Notion Service.</p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">You control your Customer Data. You determine what content and data will be uploaded to  Notion. Once Customer Data is uploaded you manage access to your workspace by allocating user logins to individuals. </p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">You also control the administration of the Customer Data by managing you groups, permissions and the user credentials that are under your control.</p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><div class="contentfulRichText_titleSpacingH3__wUQTI"><h3 id="how-does-notion-use-my-account-information" class="title_title__DWL5N title_titleSizeS__om4Io title_titleWeightSemibold__RAo21 title_titleFamilyInter__Ra6_Q"><strong class="contentfulRichText_strong__MaH0M">How does Notion use my Account Information?</strong></h3></div></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">The Notion <a href="https://www.notion.so/notion/Privacy-Policy-3468d120cf614d4c9014c09f6adc9091" class="InlineTextLink_inlineLink__oN8YM InlineTextLink_colorInherit__oGlTG">Privacy Policy</a> describes in detail how Notion collects and uses your account information.</p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><div class="contentfulRichText_titleSpacingH3__wUQTI"><h3 id="who-should-i-contact-if-i-have-any-questions-about-notion’s-data-protection-practices" class="title_title__DWL5N title_titleSizeS__om4Io title_titleWeightSemibold__RAo21 title_titleFamilyInter__Ra6_Q"><strong class="contentfulRichText_strong__MaH0M">Who should I contact if I have any questions about Notion’s data protection practices?</strong></h3></div></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">If you have any questions about our privacy practices, please contact us at:</p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">Notion Labs, Inc. 2300 Harrison Street San Francisco, CA 94110 United States <a href="mailto:privacy@makenotion.com" class="InlineTextLink_inlineLink__oN8YM InlineTextLink_colorInherit__oGlTG">privacy@makenotion.com</a></p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><div class="contentfulRichText_titleSpacingH2__yu1dl" id="gdpr"><h2 class="title_title__DWL5N title_titleSizeM__e46NM title_titleWeightBold__838EK title_titleFamilyInter__Ra6_Q"><a class="contentfulRichText_titleCursor__edkrn" href="/help/privacy#gdpr">GDPR</a><span class="contentfulRichText_permalink__tawv_"><svg class="link" viewBox="0 0 14 14" style="width:18px;height:18px;display:block;fill:inherit;flex-shrink:0"><path d="M7.03955 9.77881L7.93018 11.6978 6.28662L10.6899 7.29443C10.8774 7.72217 10.936 8.24365 10.8364 8.69482L12.5181 7.01904C13.9595 5.5835 13.9653 3.54443 12.5122 2.09131C11.0591 0.632324 9.02002 0.644043 7.58447 2.07959L5.54541 8.24072 4.96826 7.55518 4.83936Z" fill="currentColor"></path></svg></span></h2></div></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">The General Data Protection Regulation (GDPR) is a comprehensive data protection law that governs the collection of and use of personal data of EU residents, and that allows data subjects to exercise control over their data. </p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">As the GDPR is widely considered to be the most stringent global privacy standard, we have mapped our privacy program to the GDPR and other global privacy regulations.</p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><div class="contentfulRichText_titleSpacingH3__wUQTI"><h3 id="notion-as-processor-and-controller" class="title_title__DWL5N title_titleSizeS__om4Io title_titleWeightSemibold__RAo21 title_titleFamilyInter__Ra6_Q"><strong class="contentfulRichText_strong__MaH0M">Notion as Processor and Controller</strong></h3></div></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">The GDPR and other data protection legislation have two primary classifications related to the collection and processing of personal data: data controller and data processor.</p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">A data controller determines the means and purposes for processing personal data, while a data processor is a party that processes data on behalf of the data controller.</p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">Where our customer is a data controller or data processor, Notion is the data processor of personal data that our customer and their users upload to the Notion service. We process any such personal data at our customer’s direction and on our customer’s behalf. We conduct this processing in accordance with Notion’s <a href="https://www.notion.so/notion/Data-Processing-Addendum-361b540101274b1fa7e16b90402b0d99" class="InlineTextLink_inlineLink__oN8YM InlineTextLink_colorInherit__oGlTG">Data Processing Addendum</a>.</p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><div class="contentfulRichText_titleSpacingH3__wUQTI"><h3 id="cross-border-transfers-standard-contractual-clauses" class="title_title__DWL5N title_titleSizeS__om4Io title_titleWeightSemibold__RAo21 title_titleFamilyInter__Ra6_Q"><strong class="contentfulRichText_strong__MaH0M">Cross Border Transfers - Standard Contractual Clauses</strong></h3></div></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">We understand and adhere to the rules for international transfers of personal data outside of the European Economic Area and UK. </p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">In order for our customers to be confident of Notion’s data transfer processes our <a href="https://www.notion.so/notion/Data-Processing-Addendum-361b540101274b1fa7e16b90402b0d99" class="InlineTextLink_inlineLink__oN8YM InlineTextLink_colorInherit__oGlTG">Data Processing Addendum</a> incorporates both the EU and UK Standard Contractual Clauses (SCCs). In response to the Schrems II ruling, our DPA lists the technical and organisational measures we employ to ensure appropriate safeguards are in place when we transfer personal data to countries outside of the EEA and UK.  </p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">For more information about our technical security measures, please see our <a href="https://www.notion.so/security" class="InlineTextLink_inlineLink__oN8YM InlineTextLink_colorInherit__oGlTG">security page</a>.</p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><div class="contentfulRichText_titleSpacingH3__wUQTI"><h3 id="transfer-impact-assessment" class="title_title__DWL5N title_titleSizeS__om4Io title_titleWeightSemibold__RAo21 title_titleFamilyInter__Ra6_Q"><strong class="contentfulRichText_strong__MaH0M">Transfer Impact Assessment</strong></h3></div></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">Notion understands and appreciates the importance of maintaining transfer impact assessments (TIA) as a supplementary measure and as a critical piece of your privacy compliance program. </p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">To assist our customers in completing these assessments<strong class="contentfulRichText_strong__MaH0M">,</strong> we maintain <a href="https://www.notion.so/notion/Transfer-Impact-Assessment-Information-77d5463434bb4c9eb80371bb56c0f2c1" class="InlineTextLink_inlineLink__oN8YM InlineTextLink_colorInherit__oGlTG">Transfer Impact Assessment page</a> that includes all of the information about Notion that you need to complete your TIA.</p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><div class="contentfulRichText_titleSpacingH3__wUQTI"><h3 id="subprocessor-list" class="title_title__DWL5N title_titleSizeS__om4Io title_titleWeightSemibold__RAo21 title_titleFamilyInter__Ra6_Q"><strong class="contentfulRichText_strong__MaH0M">Subprocessor List</strong></h3></div></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">We work with certain companies and tool systems to provide our services to you. All of these companies have been carefully vetted for best-in-class security and data privacy practices. For more information<strong class="contentfulRichText_strong__MaH0M">,</strong> please see our <a href="https://www.notion.so/notion/Notion-s-List-of-Subprocessors-268fa5bcfa0f46b6bc29436b21676734" class="InlineTextLink_inlineLink__oN8YM InlineTextLink_colorInherit__oGlTG">list of subprocessors.</a></p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><div class="contentfulRichText_titleSpacingH2__yu1dl" id="data-governance"><h2 class="title_title__DWL5N title_titleSizeM__e46NM title_titleWeightBold__838EK title_titleFamilyInter__Ra6_Q"><a class="contentfulRichText_titleCursor__edkrn" href="/help/privacy#data-governance">Data Governance</a><span class="contentfulRichText_permalink__tawv_"><svg class="link" viewBox="0 0 14 14" style="width:18px;height:18px;display:block;fill:inherit;flex-shrink:0"><path d="M7.03955 9.77881L7.93018 8.88232C7.22705 8.81787 6.73486 8.59521 6.37158 fill="currentColor"></path></svg></span></h2></div></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">Data governance relates to the policies and procedures that dictate how data is procured and used throughout its life cycle. From creation and collection to processing, distribution, storage and deletion. </p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">Notion’s commitment to data governance is key to keeping our users data secure, private, accurate, and accessible.</p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><div class="contentfulRichText_titleSpacingH3__wUQTI"><h3 id="privacy-by-design" class="title_title__DWL5N title_titleSizeS__om4Io title_titleWeightSemibold__RAo21 title_titleFamilyInter__Ra6_Q"><strong class="contentfulRichText_strong__MaH0M">Privacy by Design</strong></h3></div></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">At Notion, we believe in privacy by design, which means that privacy considerations are built into every aspect of our products and services from the outset. This includes the development of new products, features, and the selection of vendors.</p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">Notion conducts regular training with our personnel to reinforce the concept that Notion needs to think of user privacy at all stages of the development lifecycle.</p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><div class="contentfulRichText_titleSpacingH3__wUQTI"><h3 id="data-export" class="title_title__DWL5N title_titleSizeS__om4Io title_titleWeightSemibold__RAo21 title_titleFamilyInter__Ra6_Q"><strong class="contentfulRichText_strong__MaH0M">Data Export</strong></h3></div></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">Companies generally have a duty to back up their information in multiple places. To help with this Notion offers the option to save any Notion page, database, and non-database page to your computer in various formats. This way our customers can further protect themselves by backing up their information at any time.</p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><div class="contentfulRichText_titleSpacingH3__wUQTI"><h3 id="data-import" class="title_title__DWL5N title_titleSizeS__om4Io title_titleWeightSemibold__RAo21 title_titleFamilyInter__Ra6_Q"><strong class="contentfulRichText_strong__MaH0M">Data Import</strong></h3></div></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">Notion’s data import function lets you upload information from external sources and combine it with the data already held in your workspace. </p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">Like most people, you probably have data, documents, and notes scattered across many files and apps. You can centralize your information in one place by moving it all into Notion.</p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><div class="contentfulRichText_titleSpacingH3__wUQTI"><h3 id="data-deletion" class="title_title__DWL5N title_titleSizeS__om4Io title_titleWeightSemibold__RAo21 title_titleFamilyInter__Ra6_Q"><strong class="contentfulRichText_strong__MaH0M">Data Deletion</strong></h3></div></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">The workspace owner controls the workspace’s Customer Data. This includes all of the content submitted by customers and their users. When users leave a workspace, they may have the right to request that their data is deleted by the workspace owner. When customers terminate their subscription they also have the right to request that their data be deleted by Notion.</p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">Notion allows for <a href="https://www.notion.so/help/delete-your-account" class="InlineTextLink_inlineLink__oN8YM InlineTextLink_colorInherit__oGlTG">Account Deletion</a> and <a href="https://www.notion.so/help/create-delete-and-switch-workspaces#delete-a-workspace" class="InlineTextLink_inlineLink__oN8YM InlineTextLink_colorInherit__oGlTG">Workspace Deletion</a>.</p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">When you delete an account, Notion will:</p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><ul class="contentfulRichText_list__89IEM"><li class="contentfulRichText_listItem___Swmu"><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">Delete the account associated with that email address</p></div></li><li class="contentfulRichText_listItem___Swmu"><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">Delete any <strong class="contentfulRichText_strong__MaH0M">private workspace(s) </strong>in which you are the <strong class="contentfulRichText_strong__MaH0M">only member</strong></p></div></li><li class="contentfulRichText_listItem___Swmu"><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">Delete any <strong class="contentfulRichText_strong__MaH0M">shared workspace(s) </strong>in which you are the <strong class="contentfulRichText_strong__MaH0M">only admin</strong></p></div></li><li class="contentfulRichText_listItem___Swmu"><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">Remove you from any shared workspace(s) in which you are a member or one of multiple admins</p></div></li></ul></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">To delete a workspace, you must be a workspace owner of that workspace. When you delete a workspace, Notion will:</p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><ul class="contentfulRichText_list__89IEM"><li class="contentfulRichText_listItem___Swmu"><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">Delete all content in that workspace</p></div></li><li class="contentfulRichText_listItem___Swmu"><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">Return you to another workspace you belong to, or the sign up page for Notion if you don&#x27;t belong to any others</p></div></li></ul></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">To learn more about how to delete your Notion account please see our <a href="https://www.notion.so/help/delete-your-account" class="InlineTextLink_inlineLink__oN8YM InlineTextLink_colorInherit__oGlTG">Delete Your Account</a> page. If you are a Customer and would like to terminate your contract, please see our <a href="https://www.notion.so/notion/Master-Subscription-Agreement-4e1c5dd3e3de45dfa4a8ed60f1a43da0" class="InlineTextLink_inlineLink__oN8YM InlineTextLink_colorInherit__oGlTG">MSA</a>.</p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><div class="contentfulRichText_titleSpacingH3__wUQTI"><h3 id="data-access" class="title_title__DWL5N title_titleSizeS__om4Io title_titleWeightSemibold__RAo21 title_titleFamilyInter__Ra6_Q"><strong class="contentfulRichText_strong__MaH0M">Data Access</strong></h3></div></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">Notion provides an advanced set of access functionality to help customers effectively protect their information. Notion also uses encryption to protect Customer Data from outside access.To learn more about how data access works at Notion please see our <a href="https://www.notion.so/help/data-access-consent" class="InlineTextLink_inlineLink__oN8YM InlineTextLink_colorInherit__oGlTG">Data Access Consent</a> page.</p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><div class="contentfulRichText_titleSpacingH3__wUQTI"><h3 id="data-backup" class="title_title__DWL5N title_titleSizeS__om4Io title_titleWeightSemibold__RAo21 title_titleFamilyInter__Ra6_Q"><strong class="contentfulRichText_strong__MaH0M">Data Backup</strong></h3></div></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">All Customer Data is stored in the cloud, and we keep per-minute backups of your page content on our server. That said, your data belongs to you, so we&#x27;ve made it easy to create your own backups and keep your information portable. To learn more about this please see Notion’s <a href="https://www.notion.so/help/back-up-your-data" class="InlineTextLink_inlineLink__oN8YM InlineTextLink_colorInherit__oGlTG">Back up your Data</a> page.</p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><div class="contentfulRichText_titleSpacingH2__yu1dl" id="agreements"><h2 Notion we strive to keep all of our agreements up to date with the latest regulations and industry standards. Our <a href="https://www.notion.so/Master-Subscription-Agreement-4e1c5dd3e3de45dfa4a8ed60f1a43da0" class="InlineTextLink_inlineLink__oN8YM InlineTextLink_colorInherit__oGlTG">Master Subscription Agreement</a> and<a href="https://www.notion.so/Data-Processing-Addendum-361b540101274b1fa7e16b90402b0d99" class="InlineTextLink_inlineLink__oN8YM InlineTextLink_colorInherit__oGlTG"> Data Processing Addendum</a> describe in detail Notion’s data privacy processes, standards, safeguards and our compliance with data protection legislation. </p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><p class="contentfulRichText_paragraph___hjRE">To ensure that our terms track with the GDPR, CCPA and other global privacy standards we continually have our terms assessed by leading privacy experts in multiple jurisdictions.</p></div><div class="contentfulRichText_bodyLimit__F5GOU" style="--rich-text-limit-max-width:none"><div In order to achieve this Notion maintains comprehensive and detailed policies regarding how we handle your personal information. These policies describe in detail how our users can exercise their rights with regard to their data.
